# Loinc codes are all irrelevant to Drug Substances and Drug Products.  This IG does not comply with US Core. See US Core Ticket FHIR-44844
WARNING: StructureDefinition.where(url = 'http://hl7.org/fhir/us/pq-cmc-fda/StructureDefinition/cmc-document-reference').baseDefinition: US FHIR Usage rules require that all profiles on DocumentReference derive from the core US profile. See https://confluence.hl7.org/display/CGP/US+Core+Variance+Request+Process

# National Provider Identifier (NPI), Clinical Laboratory Improvement Amendments (CLIA) Number for laboratories, and NAIC Code are not used to identify drug sponsors. See US Core Ticket FHIR-44845
WARNING: StructureDefinition.where(url = 'http://hl7.org/fhir/us/pq-cmc-fda/StructureDefinition/cmc-sponsor-organization').baseDefinition: US FHIR Usage rules require that all profiles on Organization derive from the core US profile. See https://confluence.hl7.org/display/CGP/US+Core+Variance+Request+Process

# Drug manufactures and testing sites are identified by FEI number and DUNS numbers. National Provider Identifier (NPI), Clinical Laboratory Improvement Amendments (CLIA) Number for laboratories, and NAIC Code are not used. See US Core Ticket FHIR-44846
WARNING: StructureDefinition.where(url = 'http://hl7.org/fhir/us/pq-cmc-fda/StructureDefinition/mfg-test-site-organization').baseDefinition: US FHIR Usage rules require that all profiles on Organization derive from the core US profile. See https://confluence.hl7.org/display/CGP/US+Core+Variance+Request+Process

# Supplier Organization conflicts with US Core Organization Profile on identifier codes. National Provider Identifier (NPI), Clinical Laboratory Improvement Amendments (CLIA) Number for laboratories, and NAIC Code are not used to identify drug suppliers. See US Core Ticket FHIR-44853
WARNING: StructureDefinition.where(url = 'http://hl7.org/fhir/us/pq-cmc-fda/StructureDefinition/supplier-organization').baseDefinition: US FHIR Usage rules require that all profiles on Organization derive from the core US profile. See https://confluence.hl7.org/display/CGP/US+Core+Variance+Request+Process
